  <script>
   var oid = (function(){
  var cookie = getCookie('oid');
  if(cookie){
    return cookie;
  }else{
    var new_oid = generateOid();
    setCookie('oid', new_oid, '.oricon.co.jp', '/', 'Tue, 19 Jan 2038 03:14:07 GMT', false);
    return new_oid;
  }
})();

dataLayer[0]['userId'] = oid; 
dataLayer[0]['oid'] = oid; 

function getCookie(key) {
  var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
  for (var i=0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
    var targetCookie = cookies[i];
    targetCookie = targetCookie.replace(/^¥s+|¥s+$/g, "");
    var valueIndex = targetCookie.indexOf("=");
    if (targetCookie.substring(0, valueIndex) == key) {
      return unescape(targetCookie.slice(valueIndex + 1));
    }
  }
  return "";
}

function setCookie(name, value, domain, path, expires, secure) {
  if (!name) return;
  var str = name + "=" + escape(value);
  if (domain) {
    if (domain == 1) domain = location.hostname.replace(/^[^¥.]*/, "");
    str += "; domain=" + domain;
  }
  if (path) {
    if (path == 1) path = location.pathname;
    str += "; path=" + path;
  }
  if (expires) {
    str += "; expires=" + expires;
  }
  if (secure && location.protocol == "https:") {
    str += "; secure";
  }
  document.cookie = str;
}

function generateOid() {
  var oid = "";
  var i;
  var random;
  for (i = 0; i < 32; i++) {
    random = Math.random() * 16 | 0;
    if (i == 8 || i == 12 || i == 16 || i == 20) {
      oid += "-"
    }
    oid += (i == 12 ? 4 : (i == 16 ? (random & 3 | 8) : random)).toString(16);
  }
  return oid;
}

   <script>
    $(function(){
	$(window).scroll(function(){
		var displayPos = 1180;
		var slidePos = jQuery(document).scrollTop();
		if(slidePos > displayPos){
			$('#floating-header').addClass("display");
		}else{
			$('#floating-header').removeClass("display");
		}
	})
})
   </script>
   <script>
    if(typeof current_nav_path !== "undefined" && current_nav_path){
    var path = current_nav_path;
}else{
    var path = "/";
    if(location.pathname.split("/")[1]){
        path += location.pathname.split("/")[1] + '/' ;
    }
    if(location.pathname.split("/")[1] == "category" && location.pathname.split("/")[2]){
        path += location.pathname.split("/")[2] + '/' ;
    }
}

var arr = document.getElementById("globalMenu").getElementsByTagName("a");
if(location.pathname != "/") {
    for (var i=0; i < arr.length; i++)
    {
        if(arr[i].getAttribute("href") == path){
            arr[i].className = "current";
        }			
    }
} else {
    arr[0].className = "current";
}
var arr = document.getElementById("globalMenuFloat").getElementsByTagName("a");
if(location.pathname != "/") {
    for (var i=0; i < arr.length; i++)
    {
        if(arr[i].getAttribute("href") == path){
            arr[i].className = "current";
        }			
    }
} else {
    arr[0].className = "current";
}
   </script>
